posted:Posted April 7, 2024
msg:This hotel is far from the traditional attractions in Beijing, but it is the first choice for outsiders to visit Universal Studios alone, because it is located at the "L" intersection of Beijing Capital International Airport and Universal Studios, which is very convenient for catching flights and visiting Universal Studios. For this reason, the hotel also provides guests with free shuttle buses to Universal Studios: departure at 8:30 every day, pick up guests at 20:00 for the return trip, and the one-way distance is only 7 kilometers. Tourists who think that theme park hotels are low in cost performance and young in decoration, don't hesitate, this hotel is built for you.
The hotel facilities are benchmarked against the National Five Standards, and cutting-edge facilities such as capsule coffee machines, air purifiers, smart homes, and L'Occitane toiletries are all available. Because it was opened in 2023, the hardware facilities perfectly match our concept of "living in the new, not the old".
It is 1 kilometer away from the National Grand Theater Taihu Theater, so it is called the Performing Arts Hotel. The lobby decoration with a unique artistic pedigree allows guests to feel a strong cultural a**osphere. The hotel also regularly invites students from the Communication University of Beijing to present wonderful parent-child drama performances in the hotel's supporting theater, so that guests traveling with families can enjoy a happy time of learning and entertainment.
In addition, Ctrip senior members can also upgrade their room types for free, provide welcome tea and fruits, and enjoy a more distinguished accommodation experience.
Finally, here is a guide to nearby food and movies in the hotel:
* Tongzhou is very close to Xianghe County, Hebei Province. You can order very authentic Xianghe meat pies on the takeaway platform;
* There is a Deyun Hongshi Club in the northwest of the hotel, where you can eat authentic palace dishes and the decoration is also very grand. If you want to check in, remember to make an appoin**ent one day in advance;
* There is a city avenue outside the Universal Studios Park, where you can buy souvenirs of various movie IPs without buying tickets. There is also a cinema, which not only shows new films, but also nostalgic Universal films.

msg:Great hotel outside of Universal Studios
Take your kids to Universal Studios on Saturday and book a hotel for Saturday night in advance so you can have a good night's sleep after the day's fun. Wake up naturally and then go home.
The hotel has a special shuttle bus to take tourists to Universal Studios. It departs at 8:00 in the morning and is returned to the hotel at 8:00 in the evening. After we parked the car at the hotel early in the morning, we got on the hotel bus and set off. Special thanks to the hotel staff for their flexibility. Checking in on Saturday and checking out on Sunday meant that we could have breakfast in the hotel as normal on Sunday morning. After discussing with the hotel, they agreed that we would have breakfast in the hotel the day before, which was Saturday morning.
The hotel is newly built, the lobby is spacious and bright, and the staff is very welcoming. We booked a deluxe room and the hotel upgraded it to a deluxe suite + late check-out. The breakfast I had already used was given to two more breakfasts on the second day of my stay. From this point of view, the high cost performance is on the one hand, but the enthusiasm, meticulousness and patience of the hotel manager have indeed greatly improved the guests' experience in the hotel and made them feel 100% happy.
The deluxe suite is a standard indoor and outdoor room, equipped with bar chairs, tea sets, coffee machines, and welcome fruits. The floor-to-ceiling windows are equipped with electric gauze curtains and blackout curtains. The themed sofas and VIP sofas in the outhouse are very comfortable. The bathroom in the back room is very large, with dry and wet separation.
Talking about breakfast, the quality of the breakfast here can basically meet the five-star standard. There is a Chinese food area, a cold food area, a snack area, a soup noodle area, Chinese pastries, etc. There is actually a large double-layered box filled with candies. Every area is full of care, and the food is very delicious. Friends staying here should choose the one that includes breakfast because it is worth it!
Below I will share some of my personal suggestions for hotels.
1. It is best to have tissues available inside and outside the suite.
2. The overall feel of toiletries needs to be improved, at least the packaging must be consistent. The small bottles of liquid products are very delicate.
3. Wine glasses in the suite should be prepared in advance and placed in the mini bar. This will improve the quality of the hotel equipment.
4. It would be more perfect if the guest room has two square towels for wiping hands.
5. The hotel restaurant is great, but it is recommended to have a knife because there are toast slices and butter, so a knife is still necessary.
The above is our weekend stay experience, the experience is 100%.
I hope that I can continue to maintain my original intention next time I come here.
